  <script type="467b2ded48cd09658361b355-text/javascript">
   function stickyHeader(){
 var menu = document.getElementById('header-bottom-row');
 var placeholder = document.getElementById('header-bottom-row-placeholder');
 var sticky = false;
 var topPos = 0;
 function setSticky(){
 var scrollTop = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
 if(scrollTop >= topPos){
 if(sticky){
 return;
 }else{
 menu.classList.add('sticky');
 sticky = true;
 return;
 }
 }else{
 if(sticky){
 menu.classList.remove('sticky');
 sticky = false;
 return;
 }else{
 return;
 }
 }
 }
 function init(){
 topPos = placeholder.getBoundingClientRect().top + (document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop);
 setSticky();
 }
 window.addEventListener('scroll', setSticky);
 init();
 window.addEventListener('resize', init);
 }
 stickyHeader();
 /***********************************/
  </script>
